#################
#Special Titles
#################

e_tamriel = {
	color = { 150 0 0 }

	capital = c_imperial_city
	can_be_named_after_dynasty = no

    ignore_titularity_for_title_weighting = yes
	ai_primary_priority = {
		add = @always_primary_score
	}
}

	color = { 100 0 0 }

	capital = c_volkihar

}

e_reach = {
	color = { 10 83 41 }

	capital = c_markarth
	can_be_named_after_dynasty = no
    ignore_titularity_for_title_weighting = yes
	ai_primary_priority = {
		if = {
			limit = { culture = culture:reachfolk }
			add = @correct_culture_primary_score
		}
	}
}

#Formable Cantemiris title

e_cantemiris = {
	color = { 153 131 38 }
	
	capital = c_arnesia
	can_be_named_after_dynasty = no
	ai_primary_priority = {
		if = {
			limit = { 
				culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_chimeri }
			}
			add = @correct_culture_primary_score 
		}
	}
}	

@correct_culture_primary_score = 100
@better_than_the_alternatives_score = 50
@always_primary_score = 1000

		custom_tooltip = {
			text = form_cyrodiil_lifetime_potentate
			OR = {
				# if you hold the Potentate title
				NOT = { has_title = title:e_cyrodiilic_potentate }
				# you have to either be Attrebus who fulfilled all EC tasks
				AND = {
					has_title = title:e_cyrodiilic_potentate
					has_character_flag = flag_triumphant_attrebus_twice
				}
				# or be the Potentate who defeated Attrebus and then rebuilt their realm after the collapse EK TODO: add check for Potentate for life for Aixnieras when/if those tasks are in
				AND = {
					has_title = title:e_cyrodiilic_potentate
					has_character_flag = flag_triumphant_potentate
				}
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = form_cyrodiil_legitimacy

				legitimacy_level >= 4

#formable titulars for Anequina and Pellitine, if e_Elsweyr doesn't exist

e_pellitine = {
	color = { 52 126 203 }

	capital = c_senchal

	cultural_names = {
		#Khajiit
		name_list_anequinan = cn_paalatiin
		name_list_pellitinian = cn_paalatiin
		name_list_baandari = cn_paalatiin
		#Goblins
		name_list_goblin = cn_palatina
		#Ayleid
		name_list_ayleid = cn_lattatar #Light Wood
	}

	can_be_named_after_dynasty = no
    ignore_titularity_for_title_weighting = yes
	ai_primary_priority = {
		if = {
			limit = { culture = culture:pellitinian } add = 1000
		}
	}
}

@correct_culture_primary_score = 100
@better_than_the_alternatives_score = 50
@always_primary_score = 1000

#Orsinium - formable via decision
e_orsinium = {
	color = { 100 150 70 }
	

	capital = c_old_orsinium
	can_be_named_after_dynasty = no
	ignore_titularity_for_title_weighting = yes			
	ai_primary_priority = {
		if = {
			limit = { culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_orsimeri } }
			add = @correct_culture_primary_score
		}
	}
	
	can_create = { 	
		always = no
	}
	
	k_orsinium = {
		color = { 100 150 70 }

		capital = c_old_orsinium
		can_be_named_after_dynasty = no
		ignore_titularity_for_title_weighting = yes			
		ai_primary_priority = {
			if = {
				limit = { culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_orsimeri } }
				add = @correct_culture_primary_score
			}
		}
		
		can_create = {
			culture = { has_cultural_parameter = can_found_orsinium }
		}
		
	}
}

#Formable Vvardenfell title

e_vvardenfell = {
	color = { 96 86 38 }
	
	capital = c_aldruhn
	can_be_named_after_dynasty = no
	ai_primary_priority = {
		if = {
			limit = { 
				culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_dunmeri }
				NOT = {
					faith = { has_doctrine = doctrine_pantheon_tribunal }
				}
			}
			add = @correct_culture_primary_score 
		}
	}
	
	cultural_names = {
		name_list_dwemer = cn_vthardenzel
	}
}		


@correct_culture_primary_score = 100
@better_than_the_alternatives_score = 50
@always_primary_score = 1000

#Skyrim Block
##############

###Eastern & Western Skyrim, non-formable, Skyrim Civil War 1
e_eastern_skyrim = {
	color = { 0 100 240 }
	

	capital = c_windhelm
	can_be_named_after_dynasty = no
    ignore_titularity_for_title_weighting = yes
	ai_primary_priority = {
		if = {
			limit = { culture = culture:eastmarcher }
			add = @better_than_the_alternatives_score
		}
	}
}	

e_western_skyrim = {
	color = { 0 50 125 }
	

	capital = c_solitude
	can_be_named_after_dynasty = no
    ignore_titularity_for_title_weighting = yes	
	ai_primary_priority = {
		if = {
			limit = { culture = culture:westmarcher }
			add = @better_than_the_alternatives_score
		}
	}
}

e_skyrim = {
	color = { 45 100 255 }
	

	cultural_names = {
		#aldmeris
		name_list_ayleid = cn_falmereth
		name_list_falmer = cn_falmereth
		#nede
		name_list_reachfolk = cn_marwyr #Marwyr, Mar- (above, reachspeak) -wyr (sky, from welsh)
		#goblin
		name_list_goblin = cn_skrum
	}

	#capital = c_windhelm
	can_be_named_after_dynasty = no
	ai_primary_priority = {
